{Constable_of_Jerusalem}Knights of the Holy Sepulcher
{Constable_of_Jerusalem_descr}Knight's Order of the Holy Sepulcher of Jerusalem is a catholic knight's order established by the Holy See. The origins of the Order date back to the end of the 11th - early 12th centuries. - the times when, after the First Crusade in Palestine, the Kingdom of Jerusalem arose. On the one hand, the Order relates its origins to the Christian Brotherhood of the Regular Canons, which was founded near the Temple of the Holy Sepulcher in Jerusalem in 1099, immediately after the conquest of the city by the Crusaders: The canons pursued religious goals and were responsible for protecting the pilgrims. On the other hand, the Order was the result of the religious customs of the pilgrims who wanted to be initiated into the Knights of the Holy Land. The initiation ritual was performed by the Patriarch, and later by the Franciscans Custody in the Holy Land. At the head of the Order was the King of Jerusalem, in addition, the Order was under the leadership of the Latin Patriarch of Jerusalem. The Knights of the Order were engaged in the protection of the Holy Sepulcher and other holy places of Palestine.
{Constable_of_Jerusalem_descr_short}Elite heavy cavalry, protected by heavy armor, armed with a spear for the first ramming and a mace for the melee. Unique squad

{Posaddruzhina}Posadskaya Druzhina	
{Posaddruzhina_descr}This part of the Novgorod army is subordinated to the Tyssatsky (colonel). The Novgorod Republic's vigilance system left its imprint on the essence of the position of the Tysyatsky. As well as in other ancient Russian cities, the post of the Tysyatsky grows out of the hundred-fold structure of Veliky Novgorod, but unlike other cities, the city's hundred-divided system coexists with a more organic Koncha system (dividing the city into ends and streets). Election to the post of tysyatsky takes place at the veche, which strengthens the position of the boyars, and diminishes the role of the prince in governing the state and leads to the subordination of hundreds to the citywide veche and their entry into the composition of the ends. The first Novgorodian Tysyatskys were not boyars, but were elected from their homes, and in their activity the Tysyatskys were not accountable to either the posadnik or the boyars. In this way,

The Order accepted into its ranks knights, who fell ill with leprosy. The symbol of the order is a green cross on a white cloak. The Order followed the "Charter of St. Augustine," until 1255 was not officially recognized by the Holy See, although it had certain privileges and received donations. After the capture of Jerusalem by Sulladin in October 1187, the Order took part in hostilities, particularly during the Third Crusade. In the Battle of Forbia (near Gaza) on October 17, 1244, the Order lost all its personnel. After the expulsion of the Crusaders from Palestine, the order settled in France, where he continued his hospital activities.

{Knights_Hospitaller}Hospitaller Knights
{Knights_Hospitaller_descr}The Knightly Order of St. John, also known as the Order of the Hospitallers, was created after the First Crusade. The initial task of the Hospitaller Order was to receive pilgrims in the holy land. The order provided pilgrims with lodging and medical care. The Latin word "gospital" is translated as "guest". In 1107, King Baldwin I of Jerusalem allocated land in Jerusalem to the Ionian Order (as the order was also called). At first, the Order of the Hospitallers did not engage in military operations, but over time, the monks began to guard the pilgrims. To do this, they built fortified posts and hospitals throughout Europe. In battles with Muslims, the order demonstrated its distinctive features - its soldiers were dressed in black tunics with white crosses. Frederick I Barbarossa, Holy Roman Emperor, entrusted his safety to the Knights of Saint John in a charter of privileges bestowed on the order in 1185. 
{Knights_Hospitaller_descr_short}Thanks to their training and discipline, the Hospitallers are superior to all the rest of the horsemen of the Christian world.

{Knights_Templar}Templar Knights
{Knights_Templar_descr}Knight Templar Order was created after the First Crusade to protect pilgrims traveling to the Holy Land. In the future, this award became famous for having created the world's first banking system and became immensely rich. However, the Templars were not only politicians and entrepreneurs, but valiant warriors. In 1307, by order of the Pope and the King of France, the order was dissolved, and many of its knights were arrested on charges of heresy.
{Knights_Templar_descr_short}Fearless knights guarding Christian pilgrims in the Holy Land.

{Knights_of_Antioch}St Lazarus Knights
{Knights_of_Antioch_descr}The military and Hospitaller's Order of St. Lazarus of Jerusalem was founded by the Crusaders in Palestine in 1098 on the basis of a hospital for lepers that existed under the jurisdiction of the Greek Patriarchate. The Order accepted into its ranks knights, who fell ill with leprosy. The symbol of the order is a green cross on a white cloak. The Order followed the "Charter of St. Augustine," until 1255 was not officially recognized by the Holy See, although it had certain privileges and received donations. After the capture of Jerusalem by Saladin in October 1187, the Order took part in hostilities, in particular during the Third Crusade. In the Battle of Forbia (near Gaza) on October 17, 1244, the Order lost all its personnel. After the expulsion of the Crusaders from Palestine, the order settled in France, where he continued his hospital activities.
{Knights_of_Antioch_descr_short}Vassal knights who must obey the ruler of the Principality of Antioch. They are armed with a spear, a sword and carry mail armor.

{Mutatawwi'a}Mutatawwi'a Warriors

While many Islamic volunteers are full of faith but lack the discipline and weapons, the mutatthavia units are formed from veterans of wars with infidels, heretics and other Muslims. They can afford to have chain mail, lamellar and quilted armor, supplemented by a thick shield covered with leather and iron, and strong spears. This is a military brotherhood that offers its services to any pious Muslim ruler. {NE_Monster_Ribault}Wagenburg
{NE_Monster_Ribault_descr}Wagenburgs were widely used in the Hussite wars (1419-1434). Largely thanks to combat wagons with guns mounted on them, the Hussites successfully repelled the attacks of a heavily armed enemy. The Czech version of Wagenburg was called "Tabor" or "Vozova Gradba". As a rule, the Wagenburg from combat wagons was built in the form of a quadrangle. On the side of the enemy, in front of Wagenburg, an additional ditch could be dug. Large gaps were left on the flanks for counterattacks. Artillery was installed inside the Wagenburg (if any). Light artillery and arrows took up positions directly on the carts (there were loopholes for firing in the shields). For each combat wagon, 18-21 fighters were assigned, of which there were: 4-8 crossbowmen, 2 arrows from hand bombards (in fact, they could have any available hand firearms), 6-8 fighters armed with pole arms (halberds, battle flails, etc.), 2 shield carriers and two carters. The tactics of using the Czech Wagenburg usually consisted in the fact that the Hussites first allowed the enemy to attack their fortifications. At the same time, the enemy had to go on the attack under heavy fire. Enemy cavalry (as a rule, these were heavily armed knights) could not penetrate the line of carts, and when the cavalrymen stopped in front of the carts, they were attacked directly from the carts by soldiers armed with halberds, battle flails and other pole arms. Shooters and artillery fired literally point-blank. As soon as the Hussites decided that the enemy had suffered sufficient losses and / or demoralized, their infantry and cavalry launched a counterattack. The success of the use of the Wagenburgs by the Hussites led their opponents to adopt these tactics. In the battle of Tachov (1427), the German crusaders used Wagenburg, but (apparently due to lack of experience) unsuccessfully. And in the battle of Lipan (1434), two Czech armies met: Taborites and Chasniks, each of which used Wagenburgs. At the same time, the Taborites suffered a crushing defeat; it turned out that if the enemy bursts into Wagenburg, he turns from a fortress into a deadly trap, from which there is no way out. With the death of the Taborite army, the use of the Wagenburgs in the Czech Republic ended.
{NE_Monster_Ribault_descr_short}Wagon fortifications with wooden shields and loopholes for firing

{Lendrmenn}Lendrmenn

In essence, a godendag is a combination of a club and a spear. Its design included a shaft about 150 cm long and about 10 cm in diameter at the war end, while the diameter increased throughout the entire length. The Romanovich-Mstislavich dynasty managed to preserve the traditions of the Kiev principality, however, constant interaction with its western neighbors and participation in wars and civil strife in Poland and Hungary left its mark on the branches of the armed forces, and also became the source of the appearance at the princely (and after - royal) court of the nobility with the western military traditions and equipment.
{Volyn_Knights_descr_short}Nobility of Volyn and Galych, as well as European chivalry in the service of the prince.

{Mongol_Horse_Archers_descr_short}弓骑兵在蒙古军中最为人多势 众，他们将精湛的骑射技艺融 于壹身，成为精锐轻装弓骑兵。
{Mongol_Infantry}蒙古步兵
{Mongol_Infantry_descr}素质：高级\n类型：地方兵种\n即便步下厮杀，蒙古战士 们依然军纪森严，骁勇善 战。蒙古步兵身穿轻甲， 装备长剑和强劲复合弓， 首先以强弓攒射大量杀伤 敌军，然后冲入敌阵扫荡 残余。但他们毕竟属于轻 装步兵，因此应当避免与 精锐重步兵近战肉搏。
{Mongol_Infantry_descr_short}蒙古步兵身穿轻甲，装备长剑 和强劲复合弓，颇为骁勇善战。

{Mounted_Acritae}东罗马边防骑兵
{Mounted_Acritae_descr}(Ακρίται).\n\n素质：一般\n类型：早期职业部队\n他们的名字来自于“acri ”，意思是边境。边防卫 兵负责帝国的边境戍边， 尽管是地方部队，但对他 们仍然要支付专业部队的 薪酬及给予土地。东罗马 边防卫兵配备的是帝国中 最常见的重型标枪，剑， 锁甲及头盔。

{Mounted_Arquebusiers_descr_short}改良后的火器，近战时使 用剑。
{Mounted_Calivermen}轻火枪骑兵

{Mounted_Crossbowmen}弩骑兵
{Mounted_Crossbowmen_descr}素质：一般\n类型：晚期职业部队\n面对东方来去如风的弓箭 部队，欧洲军队决意建立 更为高速机动的兵种，弩 骑兵应运而生。骑兵们使 用较步兵弩更为小巧的骑 弩，发射速度并不亚于前 者，发射后还可利用骑兵 优势，远避敌军从容装填 。

{Mounted_Longbowmen}长弓骑兵

{Mounted_Longbowmen_descr_short}骑马作战令这些长弓兵极为机 动灵活，可以从侧翼杀伤敌军， 然后迅速策马远遁，但绝对不 能令其遭遇近身搏杀。
{Mounted_Luchniki}卢日尼基弓骑兵
{Mounted_Luchniki_descr}素质：高级\n类型：晚期职业部队\n与草原民族的长期接触使 得中世纪俄国人也出现弓 骑战术。装备精良但没有 草原射手那样熟练，不能 使用环形战术。这些军队 在正式战斗之前负责侦查 和骚扰敌人。1242年亚历 山大纳夫斯基在楚德湖之 役中使用，条顿骑士惊奇 的发现自己的侧翼完全暴 露在这些弓骑兵的箭雨之 下。

{Mounted_Sergeants}骑马军士

{Musketeers}滑膛枪兵

{NE_Ballista}弩炮

{NE_Ballista_descr_short}弩炮即巨型弩弓，可发射类似 标枪的粗壮弩箭，射程极远， 能穿透敌阵。
{NE_Basilisk}蜥炮
{NE_Basilisk_descr}蜥炮乃中世纪晚期火炮设 计之巅峰之作，无论射程 、威力还是精准程度都令 先前诸多火炮自惭形秽。 任何掩体都无法抵御蜥炮 猛轰，敌军部队更是在炮 火中血肉横飞。巨蜥怪兽 的死亡凝视，令任何将领 都闻风色变。
{NE_Basilisk_descr_short}蜥炮的远程精准轰炸威力极为 惊人，对敌军防御设施和有生 力量都造成重大打击，可发射 实心或开花炮弹。
{NE_Bodyguard}早期将领卫队

{NE_Bodyguard_descr_short}将领卫队装备精良，是时刻保 护将领安危的精锐骑兵。
{NE_Bombard}攻城炮
{NE_Bombard_descr}攻城炮为最早的攻城火炮 ，于十四世纪在中国和西 欧问世，该世纪晚期迅速 传至世界各国。攻城炮炮 身由青铜或黑铁铸成，用 于发射巨型石弹摧毁敌军 防御设施，同时亦可发射 缠有易燃树脂的火球杀伤 敌军有生力量，但火球射 击精准程度不高。
{NE_Bombard_descr_short}攻城炮为最早的攻城火炮，炮 身由青铜或黑铁铸成，能发射 巨型石弹或火球，对部队射击 精准程度不高。
{NE_Cannon}加农炮
{NE_Cannon_descr}十五世纪中叶至晚期，加 农炮在世界各国军中均被 广泛使用。加农炮在轮式 炮车底盘上安置更长炮管 ，因此威力远超先前诸多 炮种，可以在更远射程上 破坏敌军防御设施，并依 靠炮弹碎片大量杀伤敌军 有生力量，威力极为恐怖 。
{NE_Cannon_descr_short}加农炮对敌军防御设施和有生 力量都能进行致命打击，可发 射实心或开花炮弹。
{NE_Catapult}投石车
{NE_Catapult_descr}投石车为木质结构，可向 敌军投掷巨石，于罗马时 期古典战争中即已大显身 手。中世纪战场上，这种 古老攻城武器逐渐为威力 更大的新式武器所取代。
{NE_Catapult_descr_short}投石车为投掷巨石的木质器械， 可投掷巨石和火球。
{NE_Culverin}长管炮
{NE_Culverin_descr}长管炮属于攻城炮种，是 极为恐怖的远程火炮，最 初出现在德国军队中。得 益于先进的冶金技术和火 炮设计，以及训练有素的 炮兵部队，长管炮无论射 程还是威力都几乎可压制 任何先前火炮。它能发射 实心或开花炮弹，既能破 坏敌军防御设施，亦可大 量杀伤敌军有生力量。
{NE_Culverin_descr_short}长管炮可发射实心或开花炮弹， 既能破坏敌军防御设施，亦可 大量杀伤敌军有生力量。
{NE_Grand_Bombard}重型攻城炮
{NE_Grand_Bombard_descr}重型攻城炮于十五世纪上 半叶问世，是对原有旧式 攻城炮的改进，其威力和 射程更为惊人。这种铁铸 火炮可对敌军防御设施造 成致命破坏，与旧式攻城 炮类似，它们亦可发射火 球以杀伤敌军有生力量。
{NE_Grand_Bombard_descr_short}与旧式攻城炮相比，重型攻城 炮无论射程、威力和精准程度 都大为提高。

{NE_Late_Bodyguard_descr_short}将领卫队自军中精锐遴选而出， 是时刻护卫将领安危的精锐骑 兵部队。
{NE_Monster_Ribault}怪兽管炮
{NE_Monster_Ribault_descr}意大利军械专家们潜心钻 研如何将更多炮管安置于 同壹炮身，最终研制成功 三十六管火炮。这种增强 管炮既能每六根炮管壹组 轮流轰击，亦可三十六根 炮管同时齐射，不愧为怪 兽之名。
{NE_Monster_Ribault_descr_short}怪兽管炮炮身上安置三十六根 炮管，可发射短程密集拦阻弹 幕。
{NE_Mortar}迫击炮
{NE_Mortar_descr}迫击炮由于形状类似臼钵 ，又名臼炮，其曲射弹道 能够避开前方障碍轰击纵 深敌军，因此既能用于攻 城作战中杀伤城中守军， 亦可在防御城邑时自城中 发射轰炸城外部队。这种 曲射攻击令迫击炮无论在 攻城或防御时都可大显身 手。
{NE_Mortar_descr_short}迫击炮的曲射弹道能够避开前 方障碍轰击纵深敌军。
{NE_Ribault}管炮
{NE_Ribault_descr}管炮又名风琴管炮，得名 于其多根炮管，是极为恐 怖的野战火炮。管炮炮身 上安置九根短程炮管，通 常在其他长程火炮掩护下 作战。九根炮管同时发射 ，令敌军冲锋部队死伤极 为惨重。
{NE_Ribault_descr_short}管炮是小型自走多管加农炮， 其九根炮管齐射，威力十分惊 人，是出色的防御火炮。
{NE_Serpentine}蛇炮
{NE_Serpentine_descr}蛇炮炮管修长，酷似巨蛇 ，故由此得名。这种火炮 基本用于杀伤敌军部队， 而非轰炸城墙。修长炮管 使蛇炮能够实施远程精确 打击，同时小口径炮弹规 格亦令炮兵装填速度更快 。
{NE_Serpentine_descr_short}蛇炮是用于专门杀伤敌军部队 而非轰击城墙的轻型加农炮。

{war_galley}加列战舰
{war_galley_descr}十一世纪始，加列战舰广 泛被地中海各国使用。与 普通加列战船相比，战舰 体积更大，吨位更重，并 安置弩炮或投石器等大型 器械。加列战舰配置大量 浆手和战士，标准海战战 术为率先击落对方船帆， 然后撞角猛击敌船，最后 接舷恶战，以定乾坤。

{Byzantine_Regular_Archers_descr}在一些装备最精良的弓 箭手队伍中，经验丰富 的弓箭手经过训练，在 射箭方面非常熟练。他 们是各省“toxicarchy”  战术步兵队形的一部分 ，也被征召来保护君士 坦丁堡的三重城墙，身 穿皮革紧身胸衣，戴着 带有棉絮或链甲的铁盔 ，或是带着皮条的酒吧 女招待。除了主要武器 ——“托克索纳”弓和 带箭的箭袋外，托索特 还有弯曲的“帕拉米隆 ”军刀。在战场上，他 们在步兵后方排成一排 ，进行大规模、非常有 针对性的射击，在远程 作战范围内比马术弓箭 手更具优势，这是通过 使用带骨垫的复合弓实 现的。
{Byzantine_Regular_Archers_descr_short}有选择的普通战士身穿 轻甲，手持剑和带骨垫 的复合弓。
{Dismounted_Latinikon}步行拉丁骑士
{Dismounted_Latinikon_descr}来自西欧的雇佣兵。这 些身披重链甲、手持剑 和盾牌的徒步战士在拜 占庭军队中扮演着非常 重要的角色。据皇帝安 娜·科姆尼娜的女儿说， 他们甚至可以攻占巴比 伦的城墙。
{Dismounted_Latinikon_descr_short}来自西欧的经验丰富的 装甲雇佣兵在拜占庭军 队中作战。带着剑和盾 牌。
{Pelikifors}瓦朗斧兵
{Pelikifors_descr}和一些雇佣兵一样，罗 马帝国成了瓦朗人的家 园。他们从罗马妇女那 里生下孩子，并继承了 用北方重型斧头砸碎头 骨的家族工艺。他们在 战斗中非常凶猛，对前 来的酒馆老板来说非常 可怕。佩利基福里亚人 自愿成为帝国的臣民， 无论如何，这给了他们 更好的标准化盔甲。每 个pelikifor都有最厚的棉 质bambakion  gambeson（可能超过1 英寸或更厚）、最高质 量的链式邮件或片状 Lorikion。他的前臂和胫 骨将分别用称 为“heiropsella”和“p odopsella”的层流护腕 和护腿进行保护。脖子 上有一个链环。
{Pelikifors_descr_short}斧头步兵
{Manglavit}帝国卫队
{Manglavit_descr}Manglavites——在翻译 中的意思是“与俱乐部 同行”这是一支由皇帝 挑选的重装步兵组成的 守卫分队，装备着大型 圆形盾牌和狼牙棒。防 守和进攻都非常有效。

{Posaddruzhina}罗斯贵族骑兵
{Posaddruzhina_descr}诺夫哥罗德军队的这一 部分隶属于蒂萨茨基（ 上校）。诺夫哥罗德共 和国的警戒系统在提西 亚茨基的立场的本质上 留下了印记。与其他俄 罗斯古代城市一样，提  西亚茨基的驿站是从维  利基·诺夫哥罗德的百倍  结构中发展而来的，但  与其他城市不同，这座  城市的百分制与一个更  有机的孔查体系共存（ 将城市分为末端和街道 ）。提西亚茨基职位的 选举在维切举行，这加 强了博雅人的地位，削 弱了王子在国家治理中 的作用，并导致数百人 从属于全市的维切人， 他们也参与了最终的组 成。第一批诺夫哥罗迪 亚人蒂希亚茨基不是博 亚尔人，而是从他们的 家中选举出来的，在他 们的活动中，蒂希亚茨 基人既不对波萨尼克人 负责，也不对博亚尔人 负责。
{Posaddruzhina_descr_short}Posadskaya druzhina （罗斯贵族）
